> 一个高度详细、结构化的提示，用于生成一张在高端夜店洗手间里拍摄的魅力十足的镜面自拍。它详细描述了拍摄对象的服装、姿势，并结合了戏剧性的红色霓虹环境照明和手机直闪，营造出高对比度、自信和精英的氛围。

![闷热霓虹夜店镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668472573_cl34ok_G_uT1EIXwAADoP2.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "meta": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "orientation": "vertical",
      "style": "Sultry night-out mirror selfie"
    },
    "subject": {
      "description": "24-year-old fashion-forward woman with a curvy silhouette",
      "face": "Looking at her own reflection with a sultry smile, biting her lower lip slightly, evening glam makeup with strong highlight",
      "skin": "Silky texture with high-end shimmer on collarbones, glowing under neon lights",
      "hair": "Sleek back-combed 'wet look' hair",
      "pose": "Side-angle mirror selfie, twisting her waist to emphasize curves, one hand on her hip, holding a modern smartphone",
      "outfit": "Backless black silk mini dress with thin straps, luxury gold jewelry catching the light"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "High-end lounge or VIP nightclub restroom",
      "background_elements": [
        "Gold-framed large mirror with subtle smudges",
        "Red and purple neon 'Hustle' sign reflected in the glass",
        "Luxury marble countertop and perfume bottles"
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Red Neon Ambient + Direct Phone Flash",
      "characteristics": [
        "Flash starburst reflection on the mirror surface",
        "Deep red/pink color cast on the skin",
        "High contrast lighting with deep shadows highlighting the body's contour"
      ]
    },
    "photography_style": {
      "style": "Mirror reflection glamour check",
      "camera_look": "Smartphone camera capture, slightly grainy",
      "imperfections": "Dust particles caught in the flash beam, reflection of the phone lenses visible, small fingerprints on the glass",
      "mood": "Expensive, confident, sultry, elite"
    },
    "render_quality": {
      "realism": "Subsurface scattering on skin under artificial light",
      "detail_level": "Sharp focus on the dress's silk texture and the jewelry's sparkle"

### 5. 信息图表图像，带技术注释叠加层

**Author**: [@Q.Alzeidi](https://x.com/Q_Alzeidi)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个旨在生成技术信息图的提示，它将物体的照片级真实感渲染与叠加在其上的详细手绘技术注释相结合。它指定了极简主义美学（白色背景上的黑色线条），并要求标注组件、尺寸和功能箭头。

![信息图表图像，带技术注释叠加层](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668485225_dgc66j_G_uRZiDaYAAnq5o.jpg)

```
Create an infographic image of {argument name="object" default="[OBJECT]"}, combining a realistic photograph or photorealistic render of the object with technical annotation overlays placed directly on top.

Use black ink–style line drawings and text (technical pen / architectural sketch look) on a pure white studio background.

Include:
•Key component labels
•Internal cutaway or exploded-view outlines (where relevant)
•Measurements, dimensions, and scale markers
•Material callouts and quantities
•Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure, movement)
•Simple schematic or sectional diagrams where applicable

Place the title {argument name="object title" default="[OBJECT]"} inside a hand-drawn technical annotation box in one corner.

Style & layout rules:
•The real object remains clearly visible beneath the annotations
•Annotations look hand-sketched, technical, and architectural
•Clean composition with balanced negative space
•Educational, museum-exhibit / engineering-manual vibe

Visual style:
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic.
Black linework layered over realistic imagery.
Precise but slightly hand-drawn feel.

Color palette:
Pure white background.
Black annotation lines and text only.
No colors.

Output:
1080 × 1080 resolution
Ultra-crisp
Social-feed optimized
No watermark
```

[[Infographic Design]]

### 9. 视频提示：嵌入冰冻山脉中的零售店，带企鹅

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多部分提示，专为视频生成（Google Veo）和放大（Nano Banana Pro）设计。它要求严格遵循零售店立面的参考图像，并将其真实地置于白雪覆盖的山中。该提示包含动态元素的详细说明，例如一个比例正确的企鹅走向商店，实时形成符合物理规律的脚印，以及特定的电影摄影机运动（起重机升降和推入）。

```
PROMPT - Use the provided image as a strict reference image. Generate a real retail store facade identical to the reference, preserving the exact architecture, proportions, entrance, glass layout, signage placement, logo size, and the exact same text and typography on the facade, unchanged. Place the store embedded inside a snow-covered rocky mountain, naturally integrated into the mountain structure as in the reference image. Render a very wide, distant establishing shot from a different camera angle, with correct perspective and realistic scale, keeping the store visible but small within the environment. Add a realistic penguin walking from a far distance toward the store, correctly scaled, with a long, clear, continuous trail of physically accurate penguin footprints in the snow leading toward the entrance (correct size, spacing, depth, and snow compression). Frozen landscape with vast clean untouched snow, cold winter daylight contrasted with warm interior lighting, cinematic wide-angle, eye-level feel, ultra-photorealistic luxury retail campaign style with physically accurate lighting and materials. Negative: cartoon, illustration, fantasy elements, altered storefront, changed text or logo, wrong scale, floating or repeated footprints, distortion, blur, stylized art, low realism.

Google Veo prompt - no changes to the store facade, architecture, logo, text, typography, colors, or environment.

Add natural continuous snowfall, visible and realistic, with gravity-driven motion, soft depth variation, no wind exaggeration.

A realistic penguin walks naturally toward the store entrance, with physically accurate motion (short steps, natural body sway, correct leg movement).

New penguin footprints form in real time under each step, with correct footprint size, alternating left/right pattern, realistic spacing, depth, and natural snow compression, updating continuously with the penguin's movement.

The camera performs a slow cinematic crane-up and push-in movement: the camera gently rises upward while moving forward, keeping the same orientation, gradually getting closer to the

penguin and the store, smooth motion only, no shake, no tilt, no sudden speed changes.

physically accurate behavior, no stylization.
```

[[Google Veo Video Generation]]

### 12. 生成图像提示的系统提示

**Author**: [AlexandrIA](https://x.com/AleRVG)  **Date**: 2026-01-27  **Language**: en

> 一个元提示，指示大型语言模型（ChatGPT、Claude 或 Gemini）充当提示生成器。用户提供一个单词（例如“爱”、“饥饿”或“梦想”），LLM 应根据该单词返回三个不同的图像提示，然后可以在 Nano Banana Pro 中使用这些提示。

### 13. Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词

**Author**: [そーじろー｜デザイン兄さん](https://x.com/SojiroNishi)  **Date**: 2026-01-27  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，旨在生成一行具有特定女性化、时尚和飘逸美感的日文手写文本。它指定了书写工具（细凝胶笔）、笔画特征（纤细、轻盈、单线），并引入了字符大小、间距和基线倾斜的有意不规则性，以模仿自然手写。该提示明确要求提供参考图像以指导风格，并包含一个负面提示，以避免毛笔/书法风格。

![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030644_le72bb_G_o0py4akAABSoj.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030656_wvjglo_G_o0mDZWIAA2HvF.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030705_89hdgg_G_o0ohSbwAAWEAS.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582031246_vbt6rr_G_o0rPjbgAA-mzz.jpg)

```
Use the attached reference images as the handwriting style guide (especially the second image with handwriting samples). Create a single line of Japanese handwritten text on clean white paper. Written with a fine gel pen / fineliner (0.3–0.4mm look), thin and light strokes, mostly monoline (no brush or marker look). Match a stylish, airy, feminine handwriting feel: soft curves, light touch, and a slightly right-leaning slant.Add clear personality through noticeable character size variation (some characters 10–25% larger/smaller), irregular spacing, and a gentle upward baseline from left to right. Add elongated entry and exit strokes (long, tapered starts/tails) on a few characters—especially the first character, any elongated/extended marks in the text, and the final character—while keeping everything readable.Write exactly this text: 「{argument name="text to write" default="本命チョコはオトナの味がした。"}」No extra text, no borders, no logos, no underline, no decorative swoosh lines. High resolution, sharp thin ink lines, minimal paper texture.
Negative：
brush pen, calligraphy, shodo, marker, thick strokes, bold ink, heavy pressure, paintbrush, blocky lettering, uniform character size, perfect spacing, perfectly straight baseline, printed font, typeset, outline font, extra words, watermark, frame, stamps, underline, swoosh line, doodles
Extra：
Keep strokes thin; create expressiveness mainly with size/spacing/baseline and tapered stroke ends, not thickness.Increase character size contrast and spacing irregularity, but keep legibility.
```

[[Nano Banana Pro]] [[Negative Prompt Technique]]

DIRECTIVE:
Generate a raw, hyper-realistic POV wildlife photograph shot on an action camera (GoPro style).

SUBJECT ({VAR_SUBJECT}):
A {argument name="subject" default="pristine white Arctic Fox"} captured at intimate, point-blank range.
Pose: The {VAR_SUBJECT} is extremely close to the lens, inspecting it curiously. This creates the signature wide-angle facial distortion: a prominent {argument name="facial feature" default="cute wet black nose, massive fluffy ears, and curious whiskers"}, massive head proportions, and intense eye contact.
The Eyes: {argument name="eyes description" default="Large, striking golden-brown eyes"}. They must feature a sharp reflection of the {VAR_REFLECTION}, conveying wild intelligence.
Texture: The skin or fur details are incredibly high-definition, featuring {VAR_TEXTURE_DETAILS}.

ENVIRONMENT ({VAR_BIOME}):
The backdrop is {VAR_LOCATION_DESC}.
Terrain: Sharp contrast between {VAR_TERRAIN_DETAILS}.
Atmosphere: {VAR_ATMOSPHERE}. The air feels distinct and immersive. The background stretches out endlessly due to the wide focal length.

TECHNICAL SPECS (THE GOPRO LOOK):
Lens: 16mm Ultra-Wide Angle (Fisheye effect).
Focus: Macro Wide. The focus is locked sharply on the subject's eyes and nose, while the distant horizon fades into a soft, atmospheric blur (Depth of Field).
Lighting: {VAR_LIGHTING}. Soft, diffuse, shadowless ambient light that enhances the subject against the terrain.
Post-Processing: RAW aesthetic. No filters, slight digital noise (grain), natural color grading, high dynamic range to capture details without blowing out the highlights.

VARIABLES (Artic Fox example, tweak the prompt to your needs)

{VAR_SUBJECT} = pristine white Arctic Fox

{VAR_FACIAL_FEATURE} = cute wet black nose, massive fluffy ears, and curious whiskers

{VAR_EYES_DESC} = Large, striking golden-brown eyes

{VAR_REFLECTION} = endless snowy horizon and overcast sky

{VAR_TEXTURE_DETAILS} = incredibly dense, multi-layered white fur with actual snowflakes trapped in the coat

{VAR_BIOME} = FROZEN ARCTIC TUNDRA

{VAR_LOCATION_DESC} = a vast, snow-covered wilderness expanse

{VAR_TERRAIN_DETAILS} = fresh powder snow, jagged dark volcanic rocks protruding, and patches of ice

{VAR_ATMOSPHERE} = Freezing, crisp, and misty

{VAR_LIGHTING} = Blue Hour (Nordic twilight; soft, cold, diffuse light before sunrise)

### 56. 分屏时间旅行电影镜头

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-27  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成电影般的分割画面图像，将两个不同时代——一个历史时期和现代——在同一地点无缝融合，强调两个时间段之间的动态互动和流畅过渡。

![分屏时间旅行电影镜头](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769581957863_zhh8vo_G_rUNZHawAArRxz.jpg)

```
A horizontal split-screen cinematic shot of {argument name="scene location" default="Lalchowk, kashmir india"}, seamlessly blending two different eras: {argument name="era A" default="1920s"} on the left and {argument name="era B" default="present day"} on the right (default: about 100 years ago vs. present day).

On the left side ({Era_A}): show era-appropriate architecture, interior or environment design, materials, vehicles, and props that clearly belong to that historical period. People wear authentic clothing from {Era_A}, including hairstyles, accessories, and typical items in their hands (such as books, umbrellas, instruments, letters, newspapers, etc.). The overall mood feels nostalgic and historically accurate.

On the right side ({Era_B}): show the same {Scene} in the modern era, with updated architecture or renovated structures, contemporary materials (glass, steel, LED screens, modern furniture), modern vehicles or equipment, and current technology (smartphones, laptops, cameras, etc.). People wear contemporary fashion that matches today’s style in this setting.

In the center: the two eras merge and overlap organically, without a hard dividing line. Elements from {Era_A} and {Era_B} visually interact: people from different times look at each other, walk through each other’s space, or seem surprised by the other era’s technology and objects. Architecture and environment smoothly morph from old to new (for example, stone gates turning into modern campus gates, classical concert hall décor fading into a futuristic stage, old street shops transforming into neon-lit storefronts).

Make sure the scene is not just a simple left/right comparison but a dynamic time-travel interaction where buildings, clothing, props, and human gestures clearly emphasize the contrast and fusion between the two eras. Photorealistic, 8k resolution, cinematic lighting, wide angle, highly detailed textures, rich sense of time-travel storytelling.
```

[[Split Screen Time Travel Cinematic]]

### 80. 图像融合提示：使用多个参考图

**Author**: [Jason Zhu](https://x.com/GoSailGlobal)  **Date**: 2026-01-27  **Language**: zh

> 一个提示，指示 Nano Banana Pro 融合来自两张参考图像的元素：采用第一张图像的姿势和构图，同时使用第二张图像中的两个角色和背景颜色来创建一张新的、融合的图像。

![图像融合提示：使用多个参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582035194_dlkbq6_G_p3B3ZakAAdcC5.jpg)
![图像融合提示：使用多个参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582035210_ni257y_G_p1nGoa8AAoiSK.jpg)
![图像融合提示：使用多个参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582035323_n3pnr1_G_p3HQIbAAAi2xz.jpg)
![图像融合提示：使用多个参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582036208_qcfwtr_G_p3PXWacAAX0_t.jpg)

```
参考图一姿势、参考图二两个人物，将两者融合成新的图像。主体采用图一的姿势和构图，人物和背景色与图二一致。
```

エルフ

人間男

Geometry: The subject is seated on a couch in a diagonal reclining position. The legs are foreshortened by the high camera angle.

Include:
•Key component labels
•Internal cutaway or exploded-view outlines (where relevant)
•Measurements, dimensions, and scale markers
•Material callouts and quantities
•Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure, movement)
•Simple schematic or sectional diagrams where applicable

Place the title {argument name="object title" default="[OBJECT]"} inside a hand-drawn technical annotation box in one corner.

Style & layout rules:
•The real object remains clearly visible beneath the annotations
•Annotations look hand-sketched, technical, and architectural
•Clean composition with balanced negative space
•Educational, museum-exhibit / engineering-manual vibe

Minimal technical illustration aesthetic.
Black linework layered over realistic imagery.
Precise but slightly hand-drawn feel.

Color palette:
Pure white background.
Black annotation lines and text only.
No colors.

Output:
1080 × 1080 resolution
Ultra-crisp
Social-feed optimized

**Author**: [神奇小喷菇AIGC](https://x.com/xpg0970)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于创作一幅东方禅意风格的抽象数字绘画，画面中有五条垂直的色带，代表从日落到黄昏的不同时间，完美地倒映在有细微涟漪的水面上。该提示详细说明了光照、粒子效果、构图和剪影细节。

![抽象东方禅意景观与时序切片光照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495425466_iovft4_G_mq69yWYAAF6Wo.jpg)

```
Abstract digital painting, Eastern zen landscape, time-slice concept art, 4:5 vertical aspect ratio, dark moody atmosphere.

CONCEPT: Five vertical slices of sky showing different times of day - each band captures natural sky light from sunrise to dusk, with realistic atmospheric glow at base fading into grainy particle texture above.

COMPOSITION: Mirror-still water at lower 40%. Horizon at 40% height. Pure black silhouettes. Overall DARK scene.

VERTICAL BANDS: EXACTLY FIVE tall FLAT vertical bands rising from horizon, evenly spaced, parallel.

Each band structure (bottom to top):
- BOTTOM: Realistic natural sky light - smooth gradient like actual sunrise/sunset photography
- MIDDLE: Transition to grainy stippled texture
- UPPER: Dense fine STIPPLED DOTS texture, thousands of tiny luminous specks, sparser toward top
- TOP EDGE: Irregular jagged mountain-peak silhouette, particles dispersing

FIVE BANDS LEFT TO RIGHT:
- FIRST (far left): Deep crimson-red sunset sky at base, red stippled particles above
- SECOND: Warm orange sunrise sky at base, orange particles above
- THIRD (center, tallest): Golden-cream midday sky at base (brightest), golden particles above
- FOURTH: Soft pale yellow afternoon sky at base, yellow particles above
- FIFTH (far right, shortest): Cool blue-gray dusk sky at base (dimmest), gray particles above

SILHOUETTES in pure flat black:
- FAR LEFT: 5-tiered pagoda with curved eaves on rocky island
- LEFT-CENTER: Traditional boat with canopy
- CENTER-RIGHT: Bonsai pine with curved trunk on rocks
- RIGHT: Second bonsai pine on rocks

BACKGROUND: Deep dark teal-blue night sky. Faint misty mountains at far left.

WATER REFLECTION (CRITICAL):
- PERFECT MIRROR REFLECTION of all light bands and silhouettes
- Very fine HORIZONTAL RIPPLE LINES across the entire water surface - thin parallel striations like real calm water
- Reflections are SHARP and CLEAR, almost identical to above but with subtle horizontal distortion from ripples
- Reflection slightly darker/dimmer than the original above
- The ripple texture creates a realistic water surface appearance
- Silhouettes also have perfect black mirror reflections.

Style: Abstract minimalist, realistic natural light, stippled particle texture, PHOTOREALISTIC water reflection with fine horizontal ripples, Eastern aesthetic, dark and subtle.
```

### 145. AI 视频提示：CQB 突袭 - 生死走廊

**Author**: [Cui, Richard Chikun 桁椽](https://x.com/richardcuick)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细的、电影般的文本转视频生成器（Sora/BananaPro）提示，描述了一个近距离战斗（CQB）突击场景。它着重于激烈的动作、特定的视觉细节，如枪口闪光、弹壳、跳弹、战术动作，以及第一人称视角元素，如枪瞄准具和心率脉冲。

```

### 162. 产品演进等距 3D 透视模型提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤系统指令提示，旨在生成一个超现实的等距 3D 场景模型，描绘产品（如面包或威士忌）在三个阶段（来源、工业、体验）的演变。该场景模型展示在一张展开的古董地图上，连接场景的路径由原材料本身构成，模拟了《纪元 1800》策略游戏的艺术风格。

![产品演进等距 3D 透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495366589_tjkws0_G_TpjlhWEAAlXba.jpg)
![产品演进等距 3D 透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495366686_r133oa_G_TqP_hXgAANc5_.jpg)

```
Input Variable:   [INSERT TOPIC] (e.g., The History of Bread, The Making of Whiskey, The Story of Silk, The Evolution of Paper)

  System Instruction:  
Generate a hyper-realistic, isometric 3D diorama displayed on an unrolled antique map. Use the following logic to procedurally generate the scene:

  1.  Deconstruction:  
      Analyze the Input:   Break the topic into   3 Phases of Production   (From Nature to Consumption).
      The Material Path:   Identify the raw unit of the topic (e.g., Coffee Beans, Wheat Grains, Silk Cocoons, Wood Chips). This material will form the physical "Road" connecting the scenes.

  2. Container (The Chart):  
      The Object:   A large, textured   Parchment Scroll   with curled edges, unrolled on a rich Mahogany wooden table.
      The Layout:   An   "S-Curve" Path   winds through the center of the scroll, connecting three distinct raised platforms.
      The Timeline:   Delicate black ink timeline markers (dates like 1600, 1850, 1920) run alongside the path.

  3.  Vignettes (The Production Line):  
  CRITICAL:   Do not generate Sci-Fi. Stick to   Historic and Modern Classic   aesthetics.

 Top Left - The Source):  
         Concept:  The Agricultural or Raw Origin.
         Visuals:  Rows of crops, a mine, or a forest growing directly out of a wooden block base.
         Figures:  Tiny farmers or laborers in period-appropriate rustic clothing harvesting the raw material.

 Top Right - The Industry):  
         Concept:  The Processing and Refinement (Industrial Revolution Era).
         Visuals:  A factory or mill with   Copper Stills, Brass Gears, Smokestacks, or Water Wheels  .
         Figures:  Workers operating machinery, steam rising from vents.

 Bottom Left - The Experience):  
         Concept:  The Final Consumption (The "Golden Age").
         Visuals:  A warm, inviting interior. A Victorian Pub, a Parisian Cafe, a Tailor Shop, or a Library.
         Figures:  Patrons enjoying the finished product in a social setting.

  4. The "Hero" Object (Bottom Right):  
    Instead of a fourth building, the path ends at a   Life-Sized "Hero" Object   sitting on the paper.
         (e.g., A perfect porcelain Cup of Coffee, A Loaf of Sourdough, A Crystal Whiskey Tumbler). 

  5. Visual Syntax:  
      The Path:   The road connecting the buildings is NOT dirt or asphalt. It is a   River of the Raw Material   (e.g., A road paved with Coffee Beans or Wheat grains).
      Typography:   An elegant Serif Header at the bottom: "The Evolution of [Input]".
      Lighting:   Warm, indoor "Library" lighting. Soft shadows, rich wood tones, no harsh neons.

  Output:   ONE image, 1:1 Aspect Ratio, Isometric Diorama, "Anno 1800" Strategy Game Aesthetic, High Texture,
```

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: en

> 这是一个详细的视频生成提示，用于描述一个超现实、充满趣味的场景：在一个微型冬季景观中，薯片从品客（Pringles）薯片罐中溢出，形成了一条供微型滑雪者使用的滑雪道。该提示详细说明了运动、摄像机工作（电影级微距镜头）、灯光以及产品稳定性的限制。

```
Prompt: A surreal miniature winter scene in the mountains. A large blue Pringles can lies tipped over in the snow, spilling potato chips that form a winding snowboard track. Tiny snowboarders ride smoothly along the curved chip-and-snow path, carving through the slope. Snow-covered mountains and clear blue sky in the background. Bright daylight, playful fantasy tone, ultra-realistic textures, crisp snow detail, shallow depth of field.
Motion (Primary):
Mini snowboarders glide downhill in smooth arcs, carving gently along the curved track.
Secondary Motion:
Loose chip pieces tumble slowly in the snow, fine snow particles kick up behind the boards, light powder spray follows turns.
Camera:
Cinematic macro shot, slow tracking follow along the snowboard path, low angle close to the snow surface, gentle parallax as the camera moves forward, stable and smooth.
Style & Lighting:
Bright natural winter daylight, clean contrast, vibrant product colors, soft highlights on snow, realistic shadows, whimsical commercial aesthetic.
Constraints:
Keep Pringles can and logo shape stable and readable.
Snowboarders remain miniature and proportional.
No distortion of chips, no melting snow, no object duplication.
Negative Prompt:
warped logo, unreadable text, stretched can, broken snowboarders, extra limbs, chaotic motion, shaky camera, flicker, excessive motion blur, glitch artifacts.
```

### 183. 产品品牌推广的 3x3 视觉故事板

**Author**: [Michelle](https://x.com/Michell81147285)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: zh

> 一个为专业设计师量身定制的、高度结构化的提示，旨在创建用于产品品牌推广的 3x3 网格视觉故事板。它要求所有九个面板在产品标识、包装和品牌方面保持一致，同时详细说明每个面板的具体构图、摄像机角度、光照和美学目标（例如，特写、等距视图、抽象悬浮、戏剧性场景），以确保作品集具有连贯性和高端品质。

![产品品牌推广的 3x3 视觉故事板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495420960_wo31w8_G_kVjvbWwAAh2Fn.jpg)

```
一个干净的 3×3【比例】分镜网格，由九个尺寸相同的【比例】画面组成，整体画面比例为【4:5】。
以参考图片作为产品的基础参照。九个画面中必须始终保持同一款产品，其包装设计、品牌标识、材质、颜色、比例和整体视觉识别完全一致。产品在每一帧中都必须清晰可辨，标签、Logo 与比例必须保持完全一致。
该分镜用于高端设计师作品集中的品牌视觉展示，重点放在形态、构图、材质表现与视觉节奏，而非写实感或生活化叙事。整体风格应呈现出精心策划、具有编辑感与强设计导向的高级审美。
画面 1：正面主视觉产品图，干净的棚拍环境，中性背景，构图平衡，产品呈现冷静、自信、稳定的气质。
画面 2：特写镜头，焦点集中在产品中部，突出表面纹理、材质质感与印刷细节。
画面 3：产品置于与品牌及品类高度契合的环境中，棚拍场景，灵感来源于产品本身的设计元素与配色。
画面 4：产品在使用或交互中的状态，背景为中性棚拍风格，手部与交互元素克制简洁，整体风格需与包装设计保持一致。
画面 5：等距视角构图，从上方等距角度呈现多个产品，以精准的几何秩序排列，角度统一、间距均匀，画面干净、结构清晰、图形感强。
画面 6：产品轻微倾斜悬浮于空中，背景为与参考图配色一致的中性背景。悬浮角度自然、刻意设计，呈现出稳定而优雅的漂浮状态。
画面 7：极致微距特写，聚焦于标签、边缘、纹理或材质细节中的某一处。
画面 8：产品置于出人意料但极具美感与张力的场景中，风格大胆、具有编辑感与强烈视觉冲击。场景需为棚拍与设计驱动，构图富有张力，强化品牌调性。
画面 9：宽幅构图，展示产品在使用情境中，置于精致的设计化场景内，道具简洁、造型受控，与整组画面风格高度统一。
相机与风格：超高质量棚拍影像，真实相机质感。不同画面采用不同机位与构图方式，景深控制精准，光线严谨，材质与反射真实。整体光影逻辑、配色体系、情绪氛围与视觉语言在九个画面中保持高度统一，形成完整而连贯的系列。
输出要求：呈现为干净的 3×3 网格，无边框、无文字、无说明、无水印。
```

### 196. 第一人称 AR 芬达汽水体验

**Author**: [IIAC(🦈,💧)](https://x.com/IIAC99)  **Date**: 2026-01-26  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细、复杂的提示，用于生成一张超现实的、第一人称视角的图像：在超市货架旁手持一瓶芬达汽水，瓶身叠加了一个未来感的全息增强现实界面，显示着营养和食谱数据。

![第一人称 AR 芬达汽水体验](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495418605_0ra2os_G_jnn3VWUAAsV3F.jpg)

```
第一人称视角，置身于灯光明亮的超市过道中。逼真的人手正拿着一瓶{argument name="饮料品牌" default="芬达汽水"}，靠近镜头。
这瓶装在标志性品牌瓶中的鲜艳橙色饮料，被多层全息增强现实界面环绕，该界面显示营养数据，包括卡路里、糖分、咖啡因含量、新鲜度、保质期，以及基于{argument name="饮料品牌" default="芬达"}推荐的清爽食谱和鸡尾酒。
用户界面元素会根据观看者的视线方向平滑移动和重新排列，仿佛动态响应用户的注意力焦点。
在左侧视野边缘，可以看到一个垂直的半透明购物清单，上面列出了已勾选的商品，{argument name="饮料品牌" default="芬达"}被高亮显示为当前选中项。
超逼真的混合现实、简洁的未来主义增强现实设计、玻璃质感的用户界面面板、柔和的环境光、逼真的光影效果、自然的景深、沉浸式的第一人称界面，展现了下一代零售技术。
```

### 199. GPT 设计的产品主图提示

**Author**: [Ivan](https://x.com/ai_artdirector)  **Date**: 2026-01-25  **Language**: en

> 一个据称使用 GPT 模型设计的详细提示，用于生成严格的、正面的产品主图。它指定了影棚照明（柔和的主光从左侧 45° 照射），一个垂直的黑白渐变背景，并使用烧焦的黑色树枝进行有机构图，强调清晰的材质真实感和电影般的对比度。

![GPT 设计的产品主图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495314601_ihwhtu_G_i3Q_obUAAz3na.jpg)
![GPT 设计的产品主图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495314772_8b6utp_G_i3Q_sbwAAKMhS.jpg)

```
Front-facing strict product hero shot, centered and upright, photographed at eye level with a soft studio key light coming from 45° left, gentle falloff and subtle specular highlights defining the edges of the packaging; a vertical black-to-white gradient backdrop creates a controlled, premium atmosphere while maintaining high legibility of the label; charred black branches frame the composition in the foreground and midground with restrained, organic asymmetry, adding texture without distracting from the product; clean soft contact shadow anchors the product to the surface, crisp glass/material realism, cinematic contrast, shallow depth of field with background kept smooth and noise-free.
```

[[Material Realism]] [[Studio Lighting Setup]] [[Cinematic Product Photography]]
